        hide_action.triggered.connect(self.hide_to_tray)
        tray_menu.addAction(hide_action)
        
        tray_menu.addSeparator()
        
        exit_action = QAction("Exit", self)
        exit_action.triggered.connect(self.clean_exit)
        tray_menu.addAction(exit_action)
        
        self.tray_icon.setContextMenu(tray_menu)
        self.tray_icon.show()
        
        # Tray icon click
        self.tray_icon.activated.connect(self._tray_icon_activated)
    
    def _start_background_updates(self):
        """Start background update timers"""
        # Status update timer
        self.status_timer = QTimer()
        self.status_timer.timeout.connect(self._update_status)
        self.status_timer.start(2000)  # Update every 2 seconds
        
        # Memory update timer
        self.memory_timer = QTimer()
        self.memory_timer.timeout.connect(self._update_memory_stats)
        self.memory_timer.start(5000)  # Update every 5 seconds
    
    # === Event Handlers ===
    
    def _process_chat_input(self):
        """Process chat input"""
        message = self.chat_input.text().strip()
        if not message:
            return
        
        # Add to chat display
        self._add_chat_message(f"You: {message}", "user")
        self.chat_input.clear()
        
        # Create task request
        task_id = f"chat_{int(time.time())}"
        request = TaskRequest(
            task_id=task_id,
            command="chat_query",
            parameters={"message": message, "context": self.chat_history[-5:]},
            source="chat_interface",
            priority=5
        )
        
        # Process in background thread
        threading.Thread(
            target=self._process_task_background,
            args=(request,),
            daemon=True
        ).start()
    
    def _process_task_background(self, request: TaskRequest):
        """Process task in background thread"""
        try:
            response = self.kernel.process_request(request)
            
            # Update UI from main thread
            self._update_chat_from_response(response)
            
            # Add to chat history
            self.chat_history.append({
                "request": request.command,
                "response": response,
                "timestamp": time.time()
            })
            
        except Exception as e:
            error_response = {
                "status": "error",
                "message": f"Processing error: {str(e)}"
            }
            self._update_chat_from_response(error_response)
    
    @Slot(dict)
    def _update_chat_from_response(self, response: dict):
        """Update chat display with response (thread-safe)"""
        if response.get("status") == "success":
            message = response.get("message", "Task completed")
            details = response.get("technical_details")
            
            display_text = f"HELENA: {message}"
            if details:
                display_text += f"\n  Details: {details}"
            
            self._add_chat_message(display_text, "helena")
        else:
            error_msg = response.get("error", response.get("message", "Unknown error"))
            self._add_chat_message(f"HELENA: Error - {error_msg}", "error")
    
    def _add_chat_message(self, message: str, sender: str):
        """Add message to chat display"""
        cursor = self.chat_display.textCursor()
        cursor.movePosition(QTextCursor.End)
        
        # Color coding
        if sender == "user":
            color = "#4A90E2"  # Blue
        elif sender == "helena":
            color = "#50C878"  # Green
        else:  # error
            color = "#FF6B6B"  # Red
        
        formatted_message = f'<span style="color:{color}">{message}</span><br>'
        
        self.chat_display.append(formatted_message)
        
        # Auto-scroll
        cursor.movePosition(QTextCursor.End)
        self.chat_display.setTextCursor(cursor)
    
    def _execute_command(self):
        """Execute console command"""
        command = self.command_input.text().strip()
        if not command:
            return
        
        # Add to console
        self._add_console_output(f"> {command}", "command")
        self.command_input.clear()
        
        # Process command
        if command.lower() == "status":
            status = self.kernel.get_system_status()
            self._add_console_output(str(status), "output")
        elif command.lower().startswith("mode "):
            new_mode = command[5:].upper()
            result = self.kernel.change_mode(new_mode)
            self._add_console_output(str(result), "output")
        elif command.lower() == "help":
            help_text = """
            Available commands:
            status - Show system status
            mode [MODE] - Change operational mode
            clear - Clear console
            help - Show this help
            """
            self._add_console_output(help_text, "output")
        elif command.lower() == "clear":
            self.console_output.clear()
        else:
            self._add_console_output(f"Unknown command: {command}", "error")
    
    def _add_console_output(self, text: str, output_type: str = "output"):
        """Add output to console"""
        cursor = self.console_output.textCursor()
        cursor.movePosition(QTextCursor.End)
        
        # Color coding
        colors = {
            "command": "#4A90E2",  # Blue
            "output": "#50C878",   # Green
            "error": "#FF6B6B",    # Red
            "system": "#FFA500"    # Orange
        }
        
        color = colors.get(output_type, "#FFFFFF")
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
        
        formatted_text = f'<span style="color:{color}">[{timestamp}] {text}</span><br>'
        
        self.console_output.append(formatted_text)
        
        # Auto-scroll
        cursor.movePosition(QTextCursor.End)
        self.console_output.setTextCursor(cursor)
    
    def _change_profile(self, profile_name: str):
        """Change performance profile"""
        try:
            profile = PerformanceProfile[profile_name]
            result = self.runtime.apply_profile(profile)
            
            # Update mode in kernel too
            if profile_name == "BACKGROUND":
                self.kernel.change_mode("background")
            elif profile_name == "IDLE":
                self.kernel.change_mode("background")
            else:
                self.kernel.change_mode("engineering")
            
            self._add_console_output(f"Profile changed to {profile_name}", "system")
            
        except Exception as e:
            self._add_console_output(f"Error changing profile: {e}", "error")
    
    def _apply_resource_limits(self):
        """Apply resource limits from controls"""
        try:
            cpu_limit = float(self.cpu_limit_input.text())
            ram_limit = float(self.ram_limit_input.text())
            
            result = self.runtime.set_operator_limits(
                cpu_percent=cpu_limit,
                ram_mb=ram_limit
            )
            
            self._add_console_output(f"Limits applied: {result}", "system")
            
        except ValueError:
            self._add_console_output("Invalid limit values", "error")
    
    def _toggle_learning(self):
        """Toggle learning mode"""
        self.kernel.learning_enabled = not self.kernel.learning_enabled
        status = "enabled" if self.kernel.learning_enabled else "disabled"
        
        self.learning_toggle.setText(f"{'Disable' if self.kernel.learning_enabled else 'Enable'} Learning")
        self._add_console_output(f"Learning {status}", "system")
    
    def _clear_cache(self):
        """Clear memory cache"""
        # Would clear actual cache in production
        self._add_console_output("Memory cache cleared", "system")
    
    def _emergency_stop(self):
        """Emergency stop button"""
        reply = QMessageBox.question(
            self, "Emergency Stop",
            "Are you sure you want to trigger emergency stop?\nThis will freeze HELENA immediately.",
            QMessageBox.Yes | QMessageBox.No
        )
        
        if reply == QMessageBox.Yes:
            self._add_console_output("EMERGENCY STOP ACTIVATED", "error")
            # In production: trigger actual emergency stop
            # self.kernel.emergency_stop()
            
            QMessageBox.warning(
                self, "System Frozen",
                "HELENA has been frozen. Manual restart required."
            )
    
    def _update_status(self):
        """Update status displays"""
        try:
            # Get kernel status
            kernel_status = self.kernel.get_system_status()
            
            # Update mode label
            self.mode_label.setText(f"Mode: {kernel_status['mode'].upper()}")
            
            # Update performance label
            avg_time = kernel_status['performance']['avg_response_time']
            self.perf_label.setText(f"Avg Response: {avg_time*1000:.0f}ms")
            
            # Update status bar
            self.statusBar().showMessage(
                f"HELENA - {kernel_status['mode'].upper()} Mode | "
                f"CPU: {kernel_status['resources']['cpu_percent']:.0f}% | "
                f"RAM: {kernel_status['resources']['memory_percent']:.0f}%"
            )
            
            # Update progress bars
            self.cpu_bar.setValue(int(kernel_status['resources']['cpu_percent']))
            self.ram_bar.setValue(int(kernel_status['resources']['memory_percent']))
            
            # Store for other use
            self.system_status = kernel_status
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error updating status: {e}")
    
    def _update_memory_stats(self):
        """Update memory statistics"""
        try:
            # This would query actual memory stats
            memory_count = len(self.memory.approved_memories)
            self.memory_stats.setText(f"Memories: {memory_count} | Cache operations")
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error updating memory stats: {e}")
    
    def _tray_icon_activated(self, reason):
        """Handle tray icon activation"""
        if reason == QSystemTrayIcon.DoubleClick:
            self.show()
            self.activateWindow()
    
    def hide_to_tray(self):
        """Hide window to system tray"""
        self.hide()
        self.is_minimized_to_tray = True
        
        # Show notification
        self.tray_icon.showMessage(
            "HELENA",
            "Running in background",
            QSystemTrayIcon.Information,
            2000
        )
    
    def closeEvent(self, event):
        """Handle window close event"""
        if self.is_minimized_to_tray:
            event.ignore()
            self.hide_to_tray()
        else:
            self.clean_exit()
    
    def clean_exit(self):
        """Clean shutdown"""
        print("Shutting down HELENA...")
        
        # Stop timers
        self.status_timer.stop()
        self.memory_timer.stop()
        
        # Shutdown runtime
        self.runtime.shutdown()
        
        # Close application
        QApplication.quit()

def main():
    """Main entry point"""
    app = QApplication(sys.argv)
    
    # Set application style
    app.setStyle('Fusion')
    
    # Create and show main window
    window = HELENADesktop()
    window.show()
    
    # Start application
    sys.exit(app.exec())

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
5. Complete Module System (With Developer API)
python
# helena_modules.py - Complete module system with DevKit
import importlib
import inspect
import hashlib
import json
import os
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Callable
from enum import Enum
import threading
import time

class ModuleStatus(Enum):
    LOADED = "loaded"
    RUNNING = "running"
    SUSPENDED = "suspended"
    ERROR = "error"
    UNLOADED = "unloaded"

class ModulePermission(Enum):
    CPU_READ = "cpu_read"
    CPU_WRITE = "cpu_write"
    MEMORY_READ = "memory_read"
    MEMORY_WRITE = "memory_write"
    NETWORK_ACCESS = "network_access"
    FILESYSTEM_READ = "filesystem_read"
    FILESYSTEM_WRITE = "filesystem_write"

@dataclass
class ModuleManifest:
    """Module metadata and requirements"""
    name: str
    version: str
    author: str
    description: str
    license: str = "HELENA-OSL-1.0"
    compatibility: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: ["HELENA >= 1.0"])
    permissions: List[ModulePermission] = field(default_factory=list)
    security_level: str = "standard"
    dependencies: Dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)

class HELENAModule(ABC):
    """Base class for all HELENA modules"""
    
    def __init__(self, api_context: 'ModuleAPI'):
        self.api = api_context
        self.manifest = self.get_manifest()
        self.status = ModuleStatus.LOADED
        self.resource_usage = ResourceTracker()
        self.last_execution = 0
        self.execution_count = 0
        
        # Validate manifest
        self._validate_manifest()
    
    @abstractmethod
    def get_manifest(self) -> ModuleManifest:
        """Return module manifest"""
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    def execute(self, task: str, parameters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Main execution method"""
        pass
    
    def initialize(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Initialize module resources"""
        self.status = ModuleStatus.RUNNING
        return {"status": "initialized", "module": self.manifest.name}
    
    def cleanup(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Cleanup module resources"""
        self.status = ModuleStatus.UNLOADED
        return {"status": "cleaned", "module": self.manifest.name}
    
    def health_check(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Check module health"""
        return {
            "module": self.manifest.name,
            "status": self.status.value,
            "execution_count": self.execution_count,
            "resource_usage": self.resource_usage.get_summary(),
            "last_execution": self.last_execution
        }
    
    def _validate_manifest(self):
        """Validate module manifest"""
        required_fields = ["name", "version", "author", "description"]
        for field in required_fields:
            if not getattr(self.manifest, field, None):
                raise ValueError(f"Missing required field in manifest: {field}")
        
        # Check for suspicious permission combinations
        if (ModulePermission.FILESYSTEM_WRITE in self.manifest.permissions and
            ModulePermission.NETWORK_ACCESS in self.manifest.permissions):
            self.api.log_warning(
                f"Module {self.manifest.name} requests both filesystem_write and network_access"
            )

class ModuleAPI:
    """API context provided to modules"""
    
    def __init__(self, module_id: str, permissions: List[ModulePermission]):
        self.module_id = module_id
        self.permissions = permissions
        self.execution_context = None
        
    def log_info(self, message: str):
        """Log info message"""
        print(f"[{self.module_id}] INFO: {message}")
    
    def log_warning(self, message: str):
        """Log warning message"""
        print(f"[{self.module_id}] WARNING: {message}")
    
    def log_error(self, message: str):
        """Log error message"""
        print(f"[{self.module_id}] ERROR: {message}")
    
    def request_permission(self, permission: ModulePermission) -> bool:
        """Request additional permission at runtime"""
        # This would trigger operator approval in production
        return False
    
    def get_system_info(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get limited system information"""
        return {
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "helena_version": "1.0.0",
            "available_memory_mb": 1024  # Placeholder
        }
    
    def call_kernel(self, command: str, parameters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Make limited kernel calls"""
        allowed_commands = ["analyze_code", "validate_syntax", "check_security"]
        
        if command not in allowed_commands:
            return {"error": f"Command not allowed: {command}"}
        
        # Placeholder for actual kernel call
        return {"status": "processed", "command": command}

class ModuleManager:
    """Manage all modules"""
    
    def __init__(self, kernel):
        self.kernel = kernel
        self.modules: Dict[str, HELENAModule] = {}
        self.module_status: Dict[str, ModuleStatus] = {}
        self.sandboxes: Dict[str, ModuleSandbox] = {}
        self.module_threads: Dict[str, threading.Thread] = {}
        
        # Load built-in modules
        self._load_builtin_modules()
    
    def _load_builtin_modules(self):
        """Load built-in modules"""
        builtins = [
            CodeAnalyzerModule,
            SecurityScannerModule,
            DocumentationGeneratorModule
        ]
        
        for module_class in builtins:
            self.load_module(module_class)
    
    def load_module(self, module_class) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Load a module class"""
        try:
            # Create API context
            module_name = module_class.__name__
            api = ModuleAPI(module_name, [])
            
            # Instantiate module
            module_instance = module_class(api)
            manifest = module_instance.manifest
            
            # Create sandbox
            sandbox = ModuleSandbox(module_instance)
            
            # Store
            self.modules[manifest.name] = module_instance
            self.module_status[manifest.name] = ModuleStatus.LOADED
            self.sandboxes[manifest.name] = sandbox
            
            # Initialize
            init_result = module_instance.initialize()
            
            print(f"Module loaded: {manifest.name} v{manifest.version}")
            
            return {
                "status": "loaded",
                "module": manifest.name,
                "version": manifest.version,
                "init_result": init_result
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error loading module {module_class}: {e}")
            return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
    
    def execute_module(self, module_name: str, task: str, 
                      parameters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Execute a module task"""
        if module_name not in self.modules:
            return {"error": f"Module not found: {module_name}"}
        
        module = self.modules[module_name]
        sandbox = self.sandboxes[module_name]
        
        # Check if module is suspended
        if self.module_status[module_name] == ModuleStatus.SUSPENDED:
            return {"error": f"Module {module_name} is suspended"}
        
        try:
            # Execute in sandbox
            result = sandbox.execute(task, parameters)
            
            # Update module stats
            module.execution_count += 1
            module.last_execution = time.time()
            
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.module_status[module_name] = ModuleStatus.ERROR
            module.api.log_error(f"Execution error: {e}")
            
            return {
                "error": str(e),
                "module": module_name,
                "task": task
            }
    
    def suspend_module(self, module_name: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Suspend a module"""
        if module_name not in self.modules:
            return {"error": f"Module not found: {module_name}"}
        
        self.module_status[module_name] = ModuleStatus.SUSPENDED
        
        # Suspend sandbox
        if module_name in self.sandboxes:
            self.sandboxes[module_name].suspend()
        
        print(f"Module suspended: {module_name}")
        return {"status": "suspended", "module": module_name}
    
    def resume_module(self, module_name: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Resume a suspended module"""
        if module_name not in self.modules:
            return {"error": f"Module not found: {module_name}"}
        
        self.module_status[module_name] = ModuleStatus.RUNNING
        
        # Resume sandbox
        if module_name in self.sandboxes:
            self.sandboxes[module_name].resume()
        
        print(f"Module resumed: {module_name}")
        return {"status": "resumed", "module": module_name}
    
    def unload_module(self, module_name: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Unload a module"""
        if module_name not in self.modules:
            return {"error": f"Module not found: {module_name}"}
        
        module = self.modules[module_name]
        
        # Cleanup
        module.cleanup()
        
        # Remove from tracking
        del self.modules[module_name]
        del self.module_status[module_name]
        
        if module_name in self.sandboxes:
            self.sandboxes[module_name].cleanup()
            del self.sandboxes[module_name]
        
        print(f"Module unloaded: {module_name}")
        return {"status": "unloaded", "module": module_name}
    
    def get_module_info(self, module_name: str = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get module information"""
        if module_name:
            if module_name not in self.modules:
                return {"error": f"Module not found: {module_name}"}
            
            module = self.modules[module_name]
            return {
                "name": module.manifest.name,
                "version": module.manifest.version,
                "author": module.manifest.author,
                "description": module.manifest.description,
                "status": self.module_status[module_name].value,
                "health": module.health_check()
            }
        else:
            # Return all modules
            return {
                "modules": {
                    name: {
                        "name": module.manifest.name,
                        "version": module.manifest.version,
                        "status": self.module_status[name].value
                    }
                    for name, module in self.modules.items()
                },
                "count": len(self.modules)
            }
    
    def auto_suspend_for_gaming(self):
        """Auto-suspend resource-intensive modules for gaming"""
        for module_name, module in self.modules.items():
            # Check if module is resource-intensive
            if module.resource_usage.average_cpu > 10:  # 10% CPU threshold
                self.suspend_module(module_name)
                print(f"Auto-suspended for gaming: {module_name}")

class ModuleSandbox:
    """Sandbox for module execution"""
    
    def __init__(self, module: HELENAModule):
        self.module = module
        self.is_suspended = False
        self.resource_monitor = ResourceMonitor()
        
    def execute(self, task: str, parameters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Execute in sandbox"""
        if self.is_suspended:
            return {"error": "Sandbox is suspended"}
        
        # Start resource monitoring
        self.resource_monitor.start()
        
        try:
            # Execute module
            result = self.module.execute(task, parameters)
            
            # Stop monitoring and update stats
            usage = self.resource_monitor.stop()
            self.module.resource_usage.update(usage)
            
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            # Still stop monitoring
            self.resource_monitor.stop()
            raise e
    
    def suspend(self):
        """Suspend sandbox"""
        self.is_suspended = True
    
    def resume(self):
        """Resume sandbox"""
        self.is_suspended = False
    
    def cleanup(self):
        """Cleanup sandbox resources"""
        self.resource_monitor.cleanup()

class ResourceTracker:
    """Track module resource usage"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.cpu_usage = []
        self.memory_usage = []
        self.execution_times = []
        self.total_executions = 0
    
    def update(self, usage: Dict[str, float]):
        """Update with new usage data"""
        self.cpu_usage.append(usage.get("cpu_percent", 0))
        self.memory_usage.append(usage.get("memory_mb", 0))
        self.execution_times.append(usage.get("execution_time", 0))
        self.total_executions += 1
        
        # Keep only last 100 measurements
        if len(self.cpu_usage) > 100:
            self.cpu_usage.pop(0)
            self.memory_usage.pop(0)
            self.execution_times.pop(0)
    
    def get_summary(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get usage summary"""
        if not self.cpu_usage:
            return {"average_cpu": 0, "average_memory": 0, "total_executions": 0}
        
        return {
            "average_cpu": sum(self.cpu_usage) / len(self.cpu_usage),
            "average_memory": sum(self.memory_usage) / len(self.memory_usage),
            "average_time": sum(self.execution_times) / len(self.execution_times),
            "total_executions": self.total_executions
        }
    
    @property
    def average_cpu(self):
        return self.get_summary()["average_cpu"]

class ResourceMonitor:
    """Monitor resource usage during execution"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.start_time = 0
        self.start_cpu = 0
        self.process = None
    
    def start(self):
        """Start monitoring"""
        self.start_time = time.time()
        self.process = psutil.Process()
        self.start_cpu = self.process.cpu_percent()
    
    def stop(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Stop monitoring and return usage"""
        if not self.process:
            return {"cpu_percent": 0, "memory_mb": 0, "execution_time": 0}
        
        execution_time = time.time() - self.start_time
        
        # Get CPU usage
        end_cpu = self.process.cpu_percent()
        cpu_percent = max(0, end_cpu - self.start_cpu)
        
        # Get memory usage
        memory_info = self.process.memory_info()
        memory_mb = memory_info.rss / (1024 * 1024)
        
        return {
            "cpu_percent": cpu_percent,
            "memory_mb": memory_mb,
            "execution_time": execution_time
        }
    
    def cleanup(self):
        """Cleanup resources"""
        self.process = None

# ===== BUILT-IN MODULES =====

class CodeAnalyzerModule(HELENAModule):
    """Built-in code analysis module"""
    
    def get_manifest(self) -> ModuleManifest:
        return ModuleManifest(
            name="CodeAnalyzer",
            version="1.0.0",
            author="HELENA Core Team",
            description="Analyzes code for quality, bugs, and optimizations",
            permissions=[ModulePermission.CPU_READ, ModulePermission.MEMORY_READ],
            security_level="trusted"
        )
    
    def execute(self, task: str, parameters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        code = parameters.get("code", "")
        language = parameters.get("language", "python")
        
        if not code:
            return {"error": "No code provided"}
        
        # Simple analysis (would be much more comprehensive in production)
        issues = []
        
        # Check for common issues
        if "import *" in code:
            issues.append({
                "type": "CODE_STYLE",
                "severity": "MEDIUM",
                "message": "Avoid 'import *' - it pollutes namespace",
                "suggestion": "Import specific functions/classes"
            })
        
        if "except:" in code or "except Exception:" in code:
            issues.append({
                "type": "ERROR_HANDLING",
                "severity": "MEDIUM",
                "message": "Bare exception handler",
                "suggestion": "Catch specific exceptions"
            })
        
        # Calculate basic metrics
        lines = code.split('\n')
        line_count = len(lines)
        comment_lines = sum(1 for line in lines if line.strip().startswith('#'))
        comment_ratio = comment_lines / line_count if line_count > 0 else 0
        
        return {
            "analysis": {
                "issues_found": len(issues),
                "line_count": line_count,
                "comment_ratio": f"{comment_ratio:.1%}",
                "language": language
            },
            "issues": issues,
            "recommendations": [
                "Run unit tests",
                "Consider adding type hints",
                "Review error handling"
            ] if not issues else ["Code looks good!"]
        }

class SecurityScannerModule(HELENAModule):
    """Built-in security scanner module"""
    
    def get_manifest(self) -> ModuleManifest:
        return ModuleManifest(
            name="SecurityScanner",
            version="1.0.0",
            author="HELENA Core Team",
            description="Scans code for security vulnerabilities",
            permissions=[ModulePermission.CPU_READ, ModulePermission.MEMORY_READ],
            security_level="trusted"
        )
    
    def execute(self, task: str, parameters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        code = parameters.get("code", "")
        
        vulnerabilities = []
        
        # Check for SQL injection patterns
        sql_patterns = ["sqlite3", "mysql.connector", "psycopg2", "execute("]
        for pattern in sql_patterns:
            if pattern in code.lower():
                # Check for string concatenation in execute
                lines = code.split('\n')
                for i, line in enumerate(lines):
                    if pattern in line.lower() and '+' in line and ('%' in line or 'format(' in line):
                        vulnerabilities.append({
                            "type": "SQL_INJECTION",
                            "severity": "CRITICAL",
                            "line": i + 1,
                            "message": "Potential SQL injection vulnerability",
                            "suggestion": "Use parameterized queries"
                        })
        
        # Check for hardcoded secrets
        secret_patterns = ["password", "secret", "key", "token", "auth"]
        lines = code.split('\n')
        for i, line in enumerate(lines):
            line_lower = line.lower()
            for pattern in secret_patterns:
                if pattern in line_lower and '=' in line and '"' in line:
                    # Check if it looks like a hardcoded value
                    if any(char.isdigit() or char.isalpha() for char in line.split('=')[1].strip(' "\'')):
                        vulnerabilities.append({
                            "type": "HARDCODED_SECRET",
                            "severity": "HIGH",
                            "line": i + 1,
                            "message": "Potential hardcoded secret",
                            "suggestion": "Use environment variables or secret management"
                        })
        
        return {
            "scan": {
                "vulnerabilities_found": len(vulnerabilities),
                "scan_time": time.time(),
                "severity_breakdown": {
                    "CRITICAL": sum(1 for v in vulnerabilities if v["severity"] == "CRITICAL"),
                    "HIGH": sum(1 for v in vulnerabilities if v["severity"] == "HIGH"),
                    "MEDIUM": sum(1 for v in vulnerabilities if v["severity"] == "MEDIUM"),
                    "LOW": sum(1 for v in vulnerabilities if v["severity"] == "LOW")
                }
            },
            "vulnerabilities": vulnerabilities,
            "summary": f"Found {len(vulnerabilities)} potential security issues"
        }

class DocumentationGeneratorModule(HELENAModule):
    """Built-in documentation generator"""
    
    def get_manifest(self) -> ModuleManifest:
        return ModuleManifest(
            name="DocumentationGenerator",
            version="1.0.0",
            author="HELENA Core Team",
            description="Generates documentation from code",
            permissions=[ModulePermission.CPU_READ],
            security_level="trusted"
        )
    
    def execute(self, task: str, parameters: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        code = parameters.get("code", "")
        
        # Extract function definitions
        lines = code.split('\n')
        functions = []
        current_function = None
        doc_lines = []
        
        for i, line in enumerate(lines):
            stripped = line.strip()
            
            # Look for function definitions
            if stripped.startswith('def '):
                if current_function:
                    functions.append(current_function)
                
                func_name = stripped[4:].split('(')[0].strip()
                current_function = {
                    "name": func_name,
                    "line": i + 1,
                    "docstring": "",
                    "params": []
                }
                
                # Try to extract parameters
                if '(' in stripped and ')' in stripped:
                    params_str = stripped.split('(', 1)[1].split(')', 1)[0]
                    params = [p.strip() for p in params_str.split(',') if p.strip()]
                    current_function["params"] = params
            
            # Look for docstrings
            elif current_function and stripped.startswith('"""'):
                # Start or end of docstring
                if not current_function["docstring"]:
                    # Start
                    docstring = stripped[3:]
                    if docstring.endswith('"""'):
                        # One-line docstring
                        current_function["docstring"] = docstring[:-3]
                    else:
                        doc_lines.append(docstring)
                else:
                    # End
                    if stripped.endswith('"""'):
                        doc_lines.append(stripped[:-3])
                    current_function["docstring"] = '\n'.join(doc_lines)
                    doc_lines = []
            
            elif doc_lines:
                # Inside docstring
                doc_lines.append(stripped)
        
        if current_function:
            functions.append(current_function)
        
        # Generate documentation
        documentation = f"# Code Documentation\n\n"
        documentation += f"Generated: {time.ctime()}\n"
        documentation += f"Total functions: {len(functions)}\n\n"
        
        for func in functions:
            documentation += f"## {func['name']}\n\n"
            documentation += f"**Location:** Line {func['line']}\n\n"
            
            if func['docstring']:
                documentation += f"**Description:** {func['docstring']}\n\n"
            
            if func['params']:
                documentation += f"**Parameters:**\n"
                for param in func['params']:
                    documentation += f"- `{param}`: \n"
                documentation += f"\n"
            
            documentation += f"---\n\n"
        
        return {
            "documentation": documentation,
            "statistics": {
                "functions_documented": len(functions),
                "functions_with_docstrings": sum(1 for f in functions if f['docstring']),
                "average_params": sum(len(f['params']) for f in functions) / max(len(functions), 1)
            },
            "note": "Documentation generated automatically. Review and edit as needed."
        }

# ===== DEVELOPER API IMPLEMENTATION =====

class DevKitAPI:
    """Complete Developer API implementation"""
    
    def __init__(self, module_manager: ModuleManager):
        self.module_manager = module_manager
        self.certification_pipeline = CertificationPipeline()
        self.marketplace = ModuleMarketplace()
        
        # API endpoints
        self.endpoints = {
            'system': self._handle_system_request,
            'modules': self._handle_module_request,
            'memory': self._handle_memory_request,
            'development': self._handle_dev_request
        }
    
    def handle_request(self, endpoint: str, method: str, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Handle API request"""
        if endpoint not in self.endpoints:
            return {"error": f"Unknown endpoint: {endpoint}"}
        
        handler = self.endpoints[endpoint]
        return handler(method, data)
    
    def _handle_system_request(self, method: str, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Handle system API requests"""
        if method == "GET":
            action = data.get("action", "status")
            
            if action == "status":
                return {
                    "system": "HELENA",
                    "version": "1.0.0",
                    "status": "operational",
                    "modules_loaded": len(self.module_manager.modules)
                }
            elif action == "resources":
                return {
                    "cpu_percent": psutil.cpu_percent(),
                    "memory_percent": psutil.virtual_memory().percent,
                    "timestamp": time.time()
                }
        
        return {"error": f"Unsupported method: {method}"}
    
    def _handle_module_request(self, method: str, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Handle module API requests"""
        if method == "GET":
            module_name = data.get("module")
            return self.module_manager.get_module_info(module_name)
        
        elif method == "POST":
            action = data.get("action")
            module_name = data.get("module")
            
            if action == "execute":
                task = data.get("task", "")
                parameters = data.get("parameters", {})
                return self.module_manager.execute_module(module_name, task, parameters)
            
            elif action == "suspend":
                return self.module_manager.suspend_module(module_name)
            
            elif action == "resume":
                return self.module_manager.resume_module(module_name)
        
        return {"error": f"Unsupported method or action: {method}/{data.get('action')}"}
    
    def _handle_memory_request(self, method: str, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Handle memory API requests"""
        # Placeholder - would interface with actual memory system
        return {
            "endpoint": "memory",
            "method": method,
            "note": "Memory API endpoints would be implemented here"
        }
    
    def _handle_dev_request(self, method: str, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Handle development API requests"""
        if method == "POST":
            action = data.get("action")
            
            if action == "certify":
                module_code = data.get("module_code")
                return self.certification_pipeline.submit_for_certification(module_code)
            
            elif action == "publish":
                module_data = data.get("module_data")
                developer_id = data.get("developer_id")
                return self.marketplace.publish_module(module_data, developer_id)
        
        return {"error": f"Unsupported development action: {data.get('action')}"}

class CertificationPipeline:
    """Module certification pipeline"""
    
    def submit_for_certification(self, module_code: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Submit module for certification"""
        # In production: full static analysis, dynamic testing, etc.
        
        # Simple checks for prototype
        checks = {
            "has_manifest": "ModuleManifest" in module_code,
            "inherits_base": "HELENAModule" in module_code,
            "no_dangerous_imports": all(danger not in module_code for danger in ["os.system", "subprocess", "__import__"]),
            "has_execute_method": "def execute" in module_code
        }
        
        passed = all(checks.values())
        
        return {
            "status": "submitted",
            "checks": checks,
            "passed": passed,
            "next_step": "human_review" if passed else "fix_issues",
            "estimated_time": "24-48 hours" if passed else "immediate_feedback"
        }

class ModuleMarketplace:
    """Module marketplace"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.listings = []
    
    def publish_module(self, module_data: Dict[str, Any], developer_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Publish module to marketplace"""
        listing_id = hashlib.sha256(
            f"{module_data.get('name')}{developer_id}{time.time()}".encode()
        ).hexdigest()[:16]
        
        listing = {
            "id": listing_id,
            "module": module_data,
            "developer": developer_id,
            "published": time.time(),
            "downloads": 0,
            "rating": 0.0
        }
        
        self.listings.append(listing)
        
        return {
            "status": "published",
            "listing_id": listing_id,
            "marketplace_url": f"marketplace.helena.ai/modules/{listing_id}",
            "note": "Module is now available in the marketplace"
        }
6. Complete Installation & Configuration Scripts
bash
#!/bin/bash
# install_helena.sh - Complete HELENA installation script

echo "HELENA AI Platform - Installation Script"
echo "========================================"

# Check Python version
PYTHON_VERSION=$(python3 --version | cut -d' ' -f2)
if [[ $(echo "$PYTHON_VERSION 3.9" | awk '{print ($1 < $2)}') -eq 1 ]]; then
    echo "ERROR: Python 3.9 or higher required. Found: $PYTHON_VERSION"
    exit 1
fi
echo "✓ Python $PYTHON_VERSION detected"

# Check dependencies
echo ""
echo "Checking system dependencies..."

# Check for pip
if ! command -v pip3 &> /dev/null; then
    echo "Installing pip..."
    python3 -m ensurepip --upgrade
fi

# Create virtual environment
echo "Creating virtual environment..."
python3 -m venv helena_env
source helena_env/bin/activate

# Install core dependencies
echo "Installing core dependencies..."
pip install --upgrade pip

# Core requirements
CORE_REQUIREMENTS=(
    "numpy>=1.21.0"
    "psutil>=5.9.0"
    "PySide6>=6.4.0"
    "cryptography>=38.0.0"
    "requests>=2.28.0"
)

pip install "${CORE_REQUIREMENTS[@]}"

# Check for GPU support
if command -v nvidia-smi &> /dev/null; then
    echo "NVIDIA GPU detected. Installing GPU support..."
    pip install "torch>=1.13.0" --index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cu117
else
    echo "Installing CPU-only PyTorch..."
    pip install "torch>=1.13.0"
fi

# Create directory structure
echo "Creating HELENA directory structure..."
mkdir -p helena_system
cd helena_system

DIRECTORIES=(
    "modules"
    "memory_store"
    "logs"
    "config"
    "cache"
    "certified_modules"
    "developer_sandboxes"
)

for dir in "${DIRECTORIES[@]}"; do
    mkdir -p "$dir"
    echo "  Created: $dir"
done

# Create configuration files
echo "Creating configuration files..."

cat > config/system_config.yaml << EOF
# HELENA System Configuration
system:
  name: "HELENA"
  version: "1.0.0"
  operator: "primary_operator"
  
performance:
  default_profile: "normal"
  auto_throttle: true
  gaming_mode_auto: true
  
memory:
  vector_dimension: 768
  max_memories: 100000
  cache_size: 1000
  
security:
  encryption_enabled: true
  require_validation: true
  max_unauthorized_attempts: 5
  
networking:
  enabled: false
  allowed_hosts: []
  require_approval: true
EOF

cat > config/module_policy.yaml << EOF
# Module Security Policy
module_security:
  default_sandbox: true
  max_cpu_percent: 25
  max_memory_mb: 512
  network_access: false
  filesystem_access: "sandbox_only"
  
certification:
  require_manual_approval: true
  automated_scanning: true
  performance_benchmark: true
  
marketplace:
  allowed_licenses:
    - "HELENA-OSL-1.0"
    - "MIT"
    - "Apache-2.0"
  minimum_rating: 4.0
  auto_updates: false
EOF

# Create startup script
cat > start_helena.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
# HELENA Startup Script

cd "$(dirname "$0")"

# Activate virtual environment
if [ -d "helena_env" ]; then
    source helena_env/bin/activate
else
    echo "Virtual environment not found. Run install_helena.sh first."
    exit 1
fi

# Check for required files
if [ ! -f "helena_desktop.py" ]; then
    echo "HELENA desktop application not found."
    exit 1
fi

# Start HELENA
echo "Starting HELENA AI Platform..."
python helena_desktop.py
EOF

chmod +x start_helena.sh

# Create service script for background operation
cat > helena_service.py << 'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
HELENA Background Service
Run this to start HELENA as a background service
"""
import sys
import os
import logging
from daemon import DaemonContext
import lockfile

# Add current directory to path
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from helena_kernel import HELENAKernel
from helena_runtime import HELENARuntime
from helena_memory import HELENAMemory

class HELENAService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.pid_file = '/tmp/helena_service.pid'
        self.log_file = './logs/service.log'
        
        # Setup logging
        logging.basicConfig(
            filename=self.log_file,
            level=logging.INFO,
            format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
        )
        self.logger = logging.getLogger('HELENA_Service')
        
    def run(self):
        """Main service loop"""
        self.logger.info("HELENA Service starting...")
        
        # Initialize core components
        kernel = HELENAKernel("service_operator")
        runtime = HELENARuntime()
        memory = HELENAMemory()
        
        # Set to background mode
        kernel.change_mode("background")
        runtime.apply_profile("background")
        
        self.logger.info("HELENA Service initialized in background mode")
        
        # Main service loop
        import time
        try:
            while True:
                # Check for tasks
                # In production: would check message queues, etc.
                time.sleep(60)  # Check every minute
                
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            self.logger.info("Service stopped by user")
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Service error: {e}")
            raise
    
    def start(self):
        """Start as daemon"""
        with DaemonContext(
            pidfile=lockfile.FileLock(self.pid_file),
            stdout=open(self.log_file, 'a+'),
            stderr=open(self.log_file, 'a+')
        ):
            self.run()
    
    def stop(self):
        """Stop daemon"""
        import signal
        import os
        if os.path.exists(self.pid_file):
            with open(self.pid_file, 'r') as f:
                pid = int(f.read().strip())
            os.kill(pid, signal.SIGTERM)
            os.remove(self.pid_file)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    service = HELENAService()
    
    if len(sys.argv) == 2:
        if sys.argv[1] == "start":
            print("Starting HELENA service...")
            service.start()
        elif sys.argv[1] == "stop":
            print("Stopping HELENA service...")
            service.stop()
        elif sys.argv[1] == "run":
            print("Running HELENA in foreground...")
            service.run()
        else:
            print(f"Unknown command: {sys.argv[1]}")
            print("Usage: helena_service.py [start|stop|run]")
    else:
        print("Usage: helena_service.py [start|stop|run]")

can you build a system that begins training HELENA once it has been setup, say, spending a set amount of time reading, training, etc. im sure you can come up with security auditing, and an inbuilt trainer to recognise feedback loops. the self improvement and software engineering systems should also be helpful to improve and cover those problems. answer, and then i will provide further ideas or prompts
We are going to design a training system for HELENA that operates under the following principles:

It is an offline-first, self-improvement system that runs on the user's hardware.

It has a set training schedule (e.g., every night, or during idle times) to read, analyze, and learn from its own experiences and provided data.

It includes security auditing to ensure that training does not compromise system integrity.

It has feedback loops to recognize and correct its own mistakes, and to improve its software engineering capabilities.

We'll design the following components:

Training Scheduler: Manages when training occurs, based on system idle time or a fixed schedule.

Data Collector: Gathers training data from HELENA's own memory, logs, and operator feedback.

Security Auditor: Validates that training data and processes are safe and do not contain malicious content.

Training Engine: The actual machine learning training process, which could involve fine-tuning a model or training a new model from scratch.

Feedback Loop Analyzer: Identifies patterns in errors and successes to improve future training.

Software Engineering Improvement System: Specifically focuses on improving coding and system optimization skills.

Since HELENA is designed to run on consumer hardware, we must be mindful of resource usage. We'll assume that training is done in the background with low priority and can be paused when the system is under load.

Let's break down each component in code.

Note: This is a high-level design. Actual implementation would require more details and integration with the existing HELENA system.

HELENA Auto-Training & Self-Improvement System
Yes, absolutely. I'll design a comprehensive self-training system that transforms HELENA from a static assistant into a continuously improving AI. This system will include autonomous learning cycles, security auditing, feedback loop recognition, and software engineering self-enhancement.
