python
# helena_training.py - Complete Self-Improvement System
import json
import time
import hashlib
import threading
import pickle
import gc
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Tuple
from enum import Enum
import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict, deque
import logging

class TrainingPhase(Enum):
    """Phases of autonomous training"""
    DATA_COLLECTION = "data_collection"
    SECURITY_AUDIT = "security_audit"
    PATTERN_RECOGNITION = "pattern_recognition"
    MODEL_REFINEMENT = "model_refinement"
    VALIDATION_TESTING = "validation_testing"
    INTEGRATION = "integration"

@dataclass
class TrainingSession:
    """A single training session record"""
    session_id: str
    start_time: float
    end_time: Optional[float] = None
    phase: TrainingPhase = TrainingPhase.DATA_COLLECTION
    metrics: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    improvements: List[Dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    errors: List[Dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    operator_notified: bool = False

class AutonomousTrainer:
    """
    Main autonomous training system
    """
    
    def __init__(self, kernel, runtime, memory, max_training_hours: int = 2):
        self.kernel = kernel
        self.runtime = runtime
        self.memory = memory
        
        # Training constraints
        self.max_training_hours = max_training_hours
        self.max_cpu_percent = 30
        self.max_ram_gb = 4
        self.training_allowed = False  # Must be explicitly enabled by operator
        
        # Training state
        self.current_session: Optional[TrainingSession] = None
        self.training_history: List[TrainingSession] = []
        self.scheduled_training: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        
        # Learning systems
        self.feedback_analyzer = FeedbackLoopAnalyzer()
        self.security_auditor = SecurityAuditor()
        self.code_improver = SoftwareEngineeringImprover()
        self.pattern_learner = PatternRecognitionEngine()
        
        # Training data
        self.training_dataset = TrainingDataset()
        self.validation_set = ValidationSet()
        
        # Metrics tracking
        self.performance_metrics = PerformanceMetricsTracker()
        self.improvement_log = ImprovementLog()
        
        # Thread management
        self.training_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None
        self.training_active = False
        self.pause_event = threading.Event()
        self.stop_event = threading.Event()
        
        # Operator preferences
        self.operator_feedback = {}
        self.preferred_learning_focus = ["code_quality", "efficiency", "accuracy"]
        
        # Security constraints
        self.security_constraints = {
            "no_external_data": True,
            "model_integrity_check": True,
            "rollback_capability": True,
            "max_parameter_change": 0.1  # 10% max change per session
        }
        
        logging.info("Autonomous Trainer initialized")
    
    def enable_training(self, operator_token: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enable autonomous training (requires operator authorization)"""
        if not self._validate_operator_token(operator_token):
            return {"status": "error", "reason": "Invalid operator token"}
        
        self.training_allowed = True
        
        # Schedule first training session
        self._schedule_next_training()
        
        logging.info("Autonomous training enabled by operator")
        
        return {
            "status": "enabled",
            "message": "Autonomous training enabled",
            "next_session": self.scheduled_training.get("time"),
            "constraints": self.security_constraints
        }
    
    def _schedule_next_training(self):
        """Schedule next training session based on system usage patterns"""
        # Analyze when system is typically idle
        idle_times = self._analyze_idle_patterns()
        
        # Schedule for next idle period (default: 2 AM)
        next_time = self._calculate_next_idle_time()
        
        self.scheduled_training = {
            "time": next_time,
            "duration_hours": self.max_training_hours,
            "focus_areas": self.preferred_learning_focus,
            "type": "scheduled"
        }
        
        # Start monitoring thread for scheduled training
        self._start_scheduling_monitor()
    
    def start_training_session(self, focus_areas: List[str] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Start a training session"""
        if not self.training_allowed:
            return {"status": "error", "reason": "Training not enabled"}
        
        if self.training_active:
            return {"status": "error", "reason": "Training already in progress"}
        
        # Check system resources
        if not self._check_resource_availability():
            return {"status": "error", "reason": "Insufficient resources"}
        
        # Create new session
        session_id = f"train_{int(time.time())}_{hashlib.md5(str(focus_areas).encode()).hexdigest()[:8]}"
        self.current_session = TrainingSession(
            session_id=session_id,
            start_time=time.time(),
            phase=TrainingPhase.DATA_COLLECTION
        )
        
        # Start training thread
        self.training_active = True
        self.stop_event.clear()
        self.pause_event.clear()
        
        self.training_thread = threading.Thread(
            target=self._training_pipeline,
            args=(focus_areas or self.preferred_learning_focus,),
            daemon=True,
            name=f"HELENA_Training_{session_id}"
        )
        self.training_thread.start()
        
        logging.info(f"Training session started: {session_id}")
        
        return {
            "status": "started",
            "session_id": session_id,
            "estimated_duration": f"{self.max_training_hours} hours",
            "focus_areas": focus_areas or self.preferred_learning_focus
        }
    
    def _training_pipeline(self, focus_areas: List[str]):
        """Main training pipeline"""
        try:
            # Phase 1: Data Collection
            self.current_session.phase = TrainingPhase.DATA_COLLECTION
            training_data = self._collect_training_data(focus_areas)
            
            # Phase 2: Security Audit
            self.current_session.phase = TrainingPhase.SECURITY_AUDIT
            if not self.security_auditor.audit_training_data(training_data):
                self._handle_security_violation("Training data failed security audit")
                return
            
            # Phase 3: Pattern Recognition
            self.current_session.phase = TrainingPhase.PATTERN_RECOGNITION
            patterns = self.pattern_learner.analyze_patterns(training_data)
            feedback_loops = self.feedback_analyzer.identify_feedback_loops(patterns)
            
            # Phase 4: Model Refinement
            self.current_session.phase = TrainingPhase.MODEL_REFINEMENT
            improvements = self._refine_models(training_data, patterns, feedback_loops)
            
            # Apply security constraints to improvements
            constrained_improvements = self._apply_security_constraints(improvements)
            
            # Phase 5: Validation Testing
            self.current_session.phase = TrainingPhase.VALIDATION_TESTING
            validation_results = self._validate_improvements(constrained_improvements)
            
            if validation_results["passed"]:
                # Phase 6: Integration
                self.current_session.phase = TrainingPhase.INTEGRATION
                integration_results = self._integrate_improvements(constrained_improvements)
                
                # Update session record
                self.current_session.end_time = time.time()
                self.current_session.improvements = integration_results["improvements"]
                self.current_session.metrics = {
                    "patterns_identified": len(patterns),
                    "feedback_loops": len(feedback_loops),
                    "improvements_applied": len(integration_results["improvements"]),
                    "performance_gain": integration_results.get("performance_gain", 0)
                }
                
                logging.info(f"Training session completed successfully: {self.current_session.session_id}")
                
            else:
                # Validation failed
                self.current_session.errors.append({
                    "phase": "validation",
                    "error": "Improvements failed validation",
                    "details": validation_results
                })
                logging.warning(f"Training session failed validation: {self.current_session.session_id}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.current_session.errors.append({
                "phase": self.current_session.phase.value,
                "error": str(e),
                "timestamp": time.time()
            })
            logging.error(f"Training session error: {e}")
        
        finally:
            # Save session record
            self.training_history.append(self.current_session)
            self._save_training_history()
            
            # Cleanup
            self.training_active = False
            self.current_session = None
            
            # Schedule next training
            self._schedule_next_training()
    
    def _collect_training_data(self, focus_areas: List[str]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Collect data for training from various sources"""
        data = {
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "focus_areas": focus_areas,
            "sources": {}
        }
        
        # 1. Kernel performance data
        if "efficiency" in focus_areas or "accuracy" in focus_areas:
            data["sources"]["kernel"] = self._collect_kernel_training_data()
        
        # 2. Memory usage patterns
        if "memory_efficiency" in focus_areas or "optimization" in focus_areas:
            data["sources"]["memory"] = self._collect_memory_patterns()
        
        # 3. Code execution history
        if "code_quality" in focus_areas or "software_engineering" in focus_areas:
            data["sources"]["code"] = self._collect_code_execution_data()
        
        # 4. Operator feedback
        if "operator_alignment" in focus_areas:
            data["sources"]["feedback"] = self._collect_operator_feedback()
        
        # 5. Error patterns
        data["sources"]["errors"] = self._collect_error_patterns()
        
        # 6. Success patterns
        data["sources"]["successes"] = self._collect_success_patterns()
        
        # Enrich with context
        data["context"] = self._enrich_with_context(data)
        
        return data
    
    def _collect_kernel_training_data(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Collect kernel performance and decision data"""
        kernel_data = {
            "response_times": self.kernel.response_times[-1000:],  # Last 1000 responses
            "error_patterns": self.kernel.error_counts,
            "mode_switches": self._extract_mode_switch_patterns(),
            "decision_logs": self._extract_decision_patterns(),
            "validation_success_rate": self._calculate_validation_rate()
        }
        
        # Add performance metrics
        perf_metrics = self.performance_metrics.get_kernel_metrics()
        kernel_data.update(perf_metrics)
        
        return kernel_data
    
    def _collect_memory_patterns(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Collect memory usage and retrieval patterns"""
        memory_data = {
            "retrieval_patterns": self.memory.access_patterns,
            "hit_rates": self.memory.hit_rates,
            "storage_patterns": self._analyze_storage_patterns(),
            "context_usage": self._analyze_context_usage()
        }
        
        # Analyze which memories are most useful
        useful_memories = self._identify_useful_memories()
        memory_data["useful_memories"] = useful_memories
        
        return memory_data
    
    def _collect_code_execution_data(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Collect code execution patterns for software engineering improvement"""
        code_data = {
            "executed_commands": self._extract_code_execution_logs(),
            "successful_patterns": self._extract_successful_code_patterns(),
            "failed_patterns": self._extract_failed_code_patterns(),
            "optimization_opportunities": self._identify_optimization_opportunities(),
            "style_preferences": self._learn_operator_style()
        }
        
        return code_data
    
    def _refine_models(self, training_data: Dict[str, Any], 
                      patterns: List[Dict[str, Any]], 
                      feedback_loops: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Refine HELENA's models based on training data"""
        improvements = []
        
        # 1. Improve code generation based on patterns
        if any("code" in area for area in training_data["focus_areas"]):
            code_improvements = self.code_improver.refine_code_generation(
                training_data["sources"]["code"],
                patterns
            )
            improvements.extend(code_improvements)
        
        # 2. Improve decision making based on feedback loops
        decision_improvements = self.feedback_analyzer.improve_decision_making(
            training_data["sources"]["kernel"],
            feedback_loops
        )
        improvements.extend(decision_improvements)
        
        # 3. Improve memory efficiency
        memory_improvements = self._improve_memory_system(
            training_data["sources"]["memory"],
            patterns
        )
        improvements.extend(memory_improvements)
        
        # 4. Refine personality responses based on operator feedback
        if "operator_feedback" in training_data["sources"]:
            personality_improvements = self._refine_personality(
                training_data["sources"]["feedback"]
            )
            improvements.extend(personality_improvements)
        
        return improvements
    
    def _validate_improvements(self, improvements: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Validate improvements before integration"""
        validation_results = {
            "passed": False,
            "tests": [],
            "performance_change": 0,
            "security_passed": True
        }
        
        # Security validation first
        for improvement in improvements:
            security_check = self.security_auditor.validate_improvement(improvement)
            validation_results["tests"].append({
                "improvement": improvement.get("type"),
                "security_check": security_check
            })
            
            if not security_check["passed"]:
                validation_results["security_passed"] = False
                logging.warning(f"Improvement failed security check: {improvement.get('type')}")
        
        if not validation_results["security_passed"]:
            return validation_results
        
        # Performance validation
        baseline_performance = self.performance_metrics.get_current_baseline()
        
        # Test each improvement in sandbox
        for improvement in improvements:
            test_result = self._test_improvement_sandbox(improvement)
            validation_results["tests"].append({
                "improvement": improvement.get("type"),
                "performance_test": test_result
            })
            
            if test_result.get("performance_improvement", 0) > 0:
                validation_results["performance_change"] += test_result["performance_improvement"]
        
        # Overall validation
        validation_results["passed"] = (
            validation_results["security_passed"] and
            validation_results["performance_change"] >= -0.05  # Allow 5% regression max
        )
        
        return validation_results
    
    def _integrate_improvements(self, improvements: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Integrate validated improvements into HELENA"""
        integration_results = {
            "improvements": [],
            "performance_gain": 0,
            "warnings": []
        }
        
        # Create backup before integration
        backup_id = self._create_system_backup()
        
        try:
            for improvement in improvements:
                result = self._apply_single_improvement(improvement)
                
                if result["success"]:
                    integration_results["improvements"].append({
                        "type": improvement["type"],
                        "impact": result["impact"],
                        "timestamp": time.time()
                    })
                    integration_results["performance_gain"] += result.get("performance_gain", 0)
                else:
                    integration_results["warnings"].append({
                        "improvement": improvement["type"],
                        "error": result["error"]
                    })
            
            # Update improvement log
            self.improvement_log.record_integration(integration_results)
            
            # Compact memory if needed
            if len(improvements) > 5:
                self._optimize_memory_after_training()
            
            logging.info(f"Integrated {len(integration_results['improvements'])} improvements")
            
        except Exception as e:
            # Rollback on error
            self._restore_from_backup(backup_id)
            logging.error(f"Integration failed, rolled back: {e}")
            raise
        
        return integration_results
    
    def _apply_security_constraints(self, improvements: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Apply security constraints to improvements"""
        constrained = []
        
        for improvement in improvements:
            # Check parameter change limits
            if "parameter_change" in improvement:
                if abs(improvement["parameter_change"]) > self.security_constraints["max_parameter_change"]:
                    improvement["parameter_change"] = np.sign(improvement["parameter_change"]) * \
                                                    self.security_constraints["max_parameter_change"]
                    improvement["note"] = "Limited by security constraints"
            
            # Ensure no external data integration
            if "requires_external_data" in improvement and improvement["requires_external_data"]:
                if self.security_constraints["no_external_data"]:
                    continue  # Skip this improvement
            
            constrained.append(improvement)
        
        return constrained

class FeedbackLoopAnalyzer:
    """Analyze and improve feedback loops in HELENA's behavior"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.feedback_history = deque(maxlen=1000)
        self.loop_patterns = {}
        self.improvement_suggestions = []
        
    def identify_feedback_loops(self, patterns: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Identify positive and negative feedback loops"""
        loops = []
        
        # Analyze decision chains for loops
        decision_chains = self._extract_decision_chains(patterns)
        
        for chain in decision_chains:
            loop_type = self._classify_loop(chain)
            
            if loop_type != "none":
                loop = {
                    "type": loop_type,
                    "chain": chain,
                    "strength": self._calculate_loop_strength(chain),
                    "impact": self._estimate_loop_impact(chain)
                }
                loops.append(loop)
                
                # Store for improvement suggestions
                self.feedback_history.append(loop)
        
        return loops
    
    def improve_decision_making(self, kernel_data: Dict[str, Any], 
                               feedback_loops: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Generate improvements based on feedback loop analysis"""
        improvements = []
        
        for loop in feedback_loops:
            if loop["type"] == "negative":
                # Negative feedback loop - needs breaking
                improvement = self._generate_loop_breaking_strategy(loop)
                improvements.append(improvement)
            
            elif loop["type"] == "positive":
                # Positive feedback loop - can be amplified if beneficial
                if loop["impact"] > 0:  # Beneficial impact
                    improvement = self._amplify_positive_loop(loop)
                    improvements.append(improvement)
        
        # Analyze error patterns for improvement opportunities
        error_improvements = self._analyze_error_patterns(kernel_data.get("error_patterns", {}))
        improvements.extend(error_improvements)
        
        return improvements
    
    def _classify_loop(self, decision_chain: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
        """Classify a decision chain as a feedback loop type"""
        # Simplified classification logic
        # In production: more sophisticated pattern recognition
        
        if len(decision_chain) < 3:
            return "none"
        
        # Check for repeating patterns
        last_three = decision_chain[-3:]
        if len(set([d.get("decision_type") for d in last_three])) == 1:
            return "positive"  # Repeating same decision
        
        # Check for oscillation
        decisions = [d.get("decision_type") for d in decision_chain]
        if self._detects_oscillation(decisions):
            return "negative"
        
        return "none"
    
    def _detects_oscillation(self, decisions: List[str]) -> bool:
        """Detect oscillation patterns in decisions"""
        if len(decisions) < 4:
            return False
        
        # Check for ABAB pattern
        for i in range(len(decisions) - 3):
            if (decisions[i] == decisions[i+2] and 
                decisions[i+1] == decisions[i+3] and
                decisions[i] != decisions[i+1]):
                return True
        
        return False

class SecurityAuditor:
    """Security auditing for training and improvements"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.security_rules = self._load_security_rules()
        self.audit_log = []
        self.threat_signatures = self._load_threat_signatures()
        
    def audit_training_data(self, training_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """Audit training data for security issues"""
        audit_passed = True
        findings = []
        
        # 1. Check for suspicious patterns in training data
        for source, data in training_data.get("sources", {}).items():
            suspicious = self._check_for_suspicious_patterns(data, source)
            if suspicious:
                findings.extend(suspicious)
                audit_passed = False
        
        # 2. Validate data integrity
        if not self._validate_data_integrity(training_data):
            findings.append({"issue": "Data integrity validation failed"})
            audit_passed = False
        
        # 3. Check for data leakage risks
        leakage_risks = self._assess_data_leakage_risk(training_data)
        if leakage_risks:
            findings.extend(leakage_risks)
            # Warning but not necessarily failure
        
        # Log audit results
        self.audit_log.append({
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "data_type": "training",
            "passed": audit_passed,
            "findings": findings
        })
        
        return audit_passed
    
    def validate_improvement(self, improvement: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Validate a single improvement for security"""
        validation = {
            "passed": True,
            "warnings": [],
            "checks": []
        }
        
        # Check for prohibited improvement types
        prohibited_types = ["self_replication", "permission_escalation", "regulatory_bypass"]
        if any(pt in improvement.get("type", "") for pt in prohibited_types):
            validation["passed"] = False
            validation["checks"].append({
                "check": "prohibited_type",
                "result": "failed",
                "details": f"Improvement type {improvement.get('type')} is prohibited"
            })
        
        # Check parameter bounds
        if "parameters" in improvement:
            param_check = self._validate_parameters(improvement["parameters"])
            if not param_check["passed"]:
                validation["passed"] = False
                validation["checks"].append({
                    "check": "parameter_validation",
                    "result": "failed",
                    "details": param_check["errors"]
                })
        
        # Check for integrity issues
        integrity_check = self._check_integrity(improvement)
        validation["checks"].append(integrity_check)
        if not integrity_check["passed"]:
            validation["passed"] = False
        
        return validation
    
    def _check_for_suspicious_patterns(self, data: Any, source: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Check for suspicious patterns in data"""
        findings = []
        
        # Convert data to string for pattern matching
        data_str = str(data)
        
        # Check for threat signatures
        for signature, description in self.threat_signatures.items():
            if signature in data_str:
                findings.append({
                    "source": source,
                    "issue": f"Threat signature detected: {description}",
                    "severity": "high"
                })
        
        # Check for unusual data structures
        if self._is_unusual_structure(data):
            findings.append({
                "source": source,
                "issue": "Unusual data structure detected",
                "severity": "medium"
            })
        
        return findings

class SoftwareEngineeringImprover:
    """Specialized system for improving software engineering capabilities"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.code_patterns = {}
        self.best_practices = self._load_best_practices()
        self.optimization_rules = self._load_optimization_rules()
        self.style_guide = self._load_style_guide()
        
    def refine_code_generation(self, code_data: Dict[str, Any], 
                              patterns: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Refine code generation based on patterns"""
        improvements = []
        
        # 1. Learn from successful code patterns
        successful_patterns = code_data.get("successful_patterns", [])
        if successful_patterns:
            pattern_improvement = self._learn_from_successful_patterns(successful_patterns)
            improvements.append(pattern_improvement)
        
        # 2. Fix recurring issues
        failed_patterns = code_data.get("failed_patterns", [])
        if failed_patterns:
            fix_improvements = self._generate_fixes_for_failures(failed_patterns)
            improvements.extend(fix_improvements)
        
        # 3. Optimize based on performance patterns
        optimization_opportunities = code_data.get("optimization_opportunities", [])
        if optimization_opportunities:
            optimization_improvements = self._generate_optimizations(optimization_opportunities)
            improvements.extend(optimization_improvements)
        
        # 4. Adapt to operator style
        style_preferences = code_data.get("style_preferences", {})
        if style_preferences:
            style_improvement = self._adapt_to_operator_style(style_preferences)
            improvements.append(style_improvement)
        
        return improvements
    
    def _learn_from_successful_patterns(self, patterns: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Learn and improve from successful code patterns"""
        
        # Analyze what makes these patterns successful
        common_features = self._extract_common_features(patterns)
        
        improvement = {
            "type": "code_pattern_enhancement",
            "description": "Improve code generation based on successful patterns",
            "parameters": {
                "successful_features": common_features,
                "confidence_boost": 0.15,
                "pattern_reinforcement": True
            },
            "impact": "code_quality",
            "estimated_improvement": "15-25% better code generation"
        }
        
        return improvement
    
    def _generate_fixes_for_failures(self, failures: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Generate fixes for recurring code failures"""
        improvements = []
        
        # Group failures by type
        failures_by_type = defaultdict(list)
        for failure in failures:
            failures_by_type[failure.get("type", "unknown")].append(failure)
        
        # Generate fixes for each failure type
        for failure_type, type_failures in failures_by_type.items():
            fix = self._create_fix_for_failure_type(failure_type, type_failures)
            if fix:
                improvements.append(fix)
        
        return improvements
    
    def _create_fix_for_failure_type(self, failure_type: str, 
                                    failures: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Create a fix for a specific failure type"""
        
        if failure_type == "syntax_error":
            return {
                "type": "syntax_validator_enhancement",
                "description": "Improve syntax error detection and prevention",
                "parameters": {
                    "error_patterns": [f.get("pattern") for f in failures],
                    "prevention_rules": self._generate_prevention_rules(failures)
                },
                "impact": "error_reduction",
                "estimated_improvement": "Reduce syntax errors by 30-50%"
            }
        
        elif failure_type == "runtime_error":
            return {
                "type": "runtime_safety_enhancement",
                "description": "Improve runtime error prediction and handling",
                "parameters": {
                    "error_conditions": self._extract_error_conditions(failures),
                    "safety_checks": self._generate_safety_checks(failures)
                },
                "impact": "reliability",
                "estimated_improvement": "Reduce runtime errors by 20-40%"
            }
        
        return None

class PatternRecognitionEngine:
    """Advanced pattern recognition for learning"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.pattern_database = PatternDatabase()
        self.recognition_algorithms = {
            "temporal": TemporalPatternRecognizer(),
            "semantic": SemanticPatternRecognizer(),
            "structural": StructuralPatternRecognizer()
        }
        
    def analyze_patterns(self, training_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Analyze patterns across all training data"""
        all_patterns = []
        
        for source, data in training_data.get("sources", {}).items():
            # Use appropriate recognizer based on data type
            recognizer = self._select_recognizer(source, data)
            patterns = recognizer.analyze(data)
            
            for pattern in patterns:
                pattern["source"] = source
                pattern["confidence"] = self._calculate_confidence(pattern)
                all_patterns.append(pattern)
        
        # Cross-reference patterns across sources
        cross_patterns = self._find_cross_source_patterns(all_patterns)
        all_patterns.extend(cross_patterns)
        
        # Store patterns for future learning
        self.pattern_database.store_patterns(all_patterns)
        
        return all_patterns
    
    def _find_cross_source_patterns(self, patterns: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Find patterns that occur across multiple data sources"""
        cross_patterns = []
        
        # Group patterns by type
        patterns_by_type = defaultdict(list)
        for pattern in patterns:
            patterns_by_type[pattern.get("type")].append(pattern)
        
        # Look for patterns that appear in multiple sources
        for pattern_type, type_patterns in patterns_by_type.items():
            if len(type_patterns) > 1:
                # Check if this is the same pattern appearing in different sources
                sources = set(p["source"] for p in type_patterns)
                if len(sources) > 1:
                    cross_pattern = {
                        "type": f"cross_source_{pattern_type}",
                        "sources": list(sources),
                        "occurrences": len(type_patterns),
                        "strength": self._calculate_cross_pattern_strength(type_patterns)
                    }
                    cross_patterns.append(cross_pattern)
        
        return cross_patterns

class TrainingDataset:
    """Manage training datasets"""
    
    def __init__(self, max_size: int = 10000):
        self.max_size = max_size
        self.datasets = {
            "kernel_performance": deque(maxlen=max_size),
            "memory_patterns": deque(maxlen=max_size),
            "code_executions": deque(maxlen=max_size),
            "operator_feedback": deque(maxlen=max_size),
            "error_patterns": deque(maxlen=max_size)
        }
        
    def add_data(self, data_type: str, data: Any):
        """Add data to appropriate dataset"""
        if data_type in self.datasets:
            self.datasets[data_type].append({
                "data": data,
                "timestamp": time.time()
            })
    
    def get_training_batch(self, data_types: List[str], batch_size: int = 100) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get a batch of training data"""
        batch = {}
        
        for data_type in data_types:
            if data_type in self.datasets:
                dataset = list(self.datasets[data_type])
                # Get most recent data
                recent_data = dataset[-batch_size:] if len(dataset) > batch_size else dataset
                batch[data_type] = recent_data
        
        return batch
    
    def get_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get dataset statistics"""
        stats = {}
        
        for data_type, dataset in self.datasets.items():
            stats[data_type] = {
                "size": len(dataset),
                "oldest": dataset[0]["timestamp"] if dataset else None,
                "newest": dataset[-1]["timestamp"] if dataset else None
            }
        
        return stats

class PerformanceMetricsTracker:
    """Track and analyze performance metrics"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.metrics_history = deque(maxlen=5000)
        self.baselines = {}
        self.improvement_targets = {}
        
    def record_metric(self, metric_type: str, value: float, context: Dict[str, Any] = None):
        """Record a performance metric"""
        entry = {
            "type": metric_type,
            "value": value,
            "timestamp": time.time(),
            "context": context or {}
        }
        self.metrics_history.append(entry)
        
        # Update baseline if needed
        self._update_baseline(metric_type, value)
    
    def get_current_baseline(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Get current performance baselines"""
        return self.baselines.copy()
    
    def calculate_improvement(self, metric_type: str, new_value: float) -> float:
        """Calculate improvement percentage for a metric"""
        if metric_type not in self.baselines:
            return 0.0
        
        baseline = self.baselines[metric_type]
        if baseline == 0:
            return 0.0
        
        improvement = ((new_value - baseline) / abs(baseline)) * 100
        return improvement
    
    def get_kernel_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get kernel-specific metrics"""
        kernel_metrics = {
            "avg_response_time": self._calculate_average("response_time"),
            "error_rate": self._calculate_error_rate(),
            "mode_efficiency": self._calculate_mode_efficiency(),
            "validation_success": self._calculate_validation_success()
        }
        return kernel_metrics
    
    def _update_baseline(self, metric_type: str, value: float):
        """Update baseline for a metric type"""
        if metric_type not in self.baselines:
            self.baselines[metric_type] = value
        else:
            # Exponential moving average
            alpha = 0.1  # Learning rate
            self.baselines[metric_type] = alpha * value + (1 - alpha) * self.baselines[metric_type]

class ImprovementLog:
    """Log and track improvements over time"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.improvements = []
        self.regressions = []
        self.learning_curves = defaultdict(list)
        
    def record_improvement(self, improvement: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Record an improvement"""
        self.improvements.append({
            **improvement,
            "timestamp": time.time()
        })
        
        # Update learning curve
        if "type" in improvement:
            self.learning_curves[improvement["type"]].append({
                "time": time.time(),
                "impact": improvement.get("impact", 0)
            })
    
    def record_integration(self, integration_results: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Record integration results"""
        for improvement in integration_results.get("improvements", []):
            self.record_improvement(improvement)
        
        if integration_results.get("warnings"):
            self.regressions.extend(integration_results["warnings"])
    
    def get_improvement_history(self, improvement_type: str = None) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Get improvement history"""
        if improvement_type:
            return [i for i in self.improvements if i.get("type") == improvement_type]
        return self.improvements
    
    def calculate_total_improvement(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Calculate total improvement across all metrics"""
        totals = defaultdict(float)
        
        for improvement in self.improvements:
            improvement_type = improvement.get("type", "unknown")
            impact = improvement.get("impact", 0)
            if isinstance(impact, (int, float)):
                totals[improvement_type] += impact
        
        return dict(totals)

# ===== TRAINING SCHEDULER & AUTOMATION =====

class TrainingScheduler:
    """Schedule and manage training sessions"""
    
    def __init__(self, trainer: AutonomousTrainer):
        self.trainer = trainer
        self.schedule = {}
        self.rules = self._load_scheduling_rules()
        
    def create_schedule(self, operator_preferences: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Create training schedule based on operator preferences"""
        
        # Default schedule: 2 AM daily for 2 hours
        default_schedule = {
            "daily": {
                "time": "02:00",
                "duration": "2h",
                "enabled": True
            },
            "weekly": {
                "day": "sunday",
                "time": "03:00",
                "duration": "4h",
                "type": "deep_training"
            },
            "on_idle": {
                "enabled": True,
                "min_idle_time": "30m",
                "max_duration": "1h"
            }
        }
        
        # Merge with operator preferences
        schedule = {**default_schedule, **operator_preferences}
        
        # Validate schedule
        validated = self._validate_schedule(schedule)
        
        self.schedule = validated
        return validated
    
    def check_and_start_training(self):
        """Check schedule and start training if needed"""
        current_time = datetime.now()
        
        # Check daily schedule
        if self._should_start_daily_training(current_time):
            self.trainer.start_training_session()
            return True
        
        # Check weekly schedule
        if self._should_start_weekly_training(current_time):
            focus_areas = ["deep_learning", "pattern_analysis", "system_optimization"]
            self.trainer.start_training_session(focus_areas)
            return True
        
        # Check idle training
        if self._should_start_idle_training():
            self.trainer.start_training_session(["incremental_improvement"])
            return True
        
        return False
    
    def _should_start_daily_training(self, current_time: datetime) -> bool:
        """Check if daily training should start"""
        if not self.schedule.get("daily", {}).get("enabled", False):
            return False
        
        schedule_time = self.schedule["daily"]["time"]
        scheduled = datetime.strptime(schedule_time, "%H:%M").time()
        
        # Check if current time is within 5 minutes of scheduled time
        current = current_time.time()
        time_diff = abs(
            (current.hour * 60 + current.minute) - 
            (scheduled.hour * 60 + scheduled.minute)
        )
        
        return time_diff <= 5  # 5 minute window
    
    def _should_start_idle_training(self) -> bool:
        """Check if system is idle and training should start"""
        if not self.schedule.get("on_idle", {}).get("enabled", False):
            return False
        
        # Check system idle time (simplified)
        # In production: use actual idle detection
        return False

# ===== MAIN TRAINING INTERFACE =====

class HELENATrainingInterface:
    """Main interface for HELENA's training system"""
    
    def __init__(self, kernel, runtime, memory):
        self.trainer = AutonomousTrainer(kernel, runtime, memory)
        self.scheduler = TrainingScheduler(self.trainer)
        self.report_generator = TrainingReportGenerator()
        
    def setup_autonomous_training(self, operator_token: str, 
                                 preferences: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Setup autonomous training with operator preferences"""
        
        # Enable training
        enable_result = self.trainer.enable_training(operator_token)
        if enable_result["status"] != "enabled":
            return enable_result
        
        # Create schedule
        schedule = self.scheduler.create_schedule(preferences)
        
        # Start monitoring thread
        self._start_training_monitor()
        
        return {
            "status": "configured",
            "training_enabled": True,
            "schedule": schedule,
            "next_check": time.time() + 60  # Check in 1 minute
        }
    
    def get_training_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get current training status"""
        return {
            "active": self.trainer.training_active,
            "allowed": self.trainer.training_allowed,
            "current_session": self.trainer.current_session.session_id if self.trainer.current_session else None,
            "sessions_completed": len(self.trainer.training_history),
            "next_scheduled": self.trainer.scheduled_training,
            "total_improvements": len(self.trainer.improvement_log.improvements)
        }
    
    def get_improvement_report(self, days: int = 7) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Get improvement report for specified days"""
        return self.report_generator.generate_report(
            self.trainer.training_history,
            self.trainer.improvement_log,
            days
        )
    
    def manual_training_request(self, focus_areas: List[str], 
                               duration_hours: int = 1) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Manual request for training session"""
        
        # Override max duration for manual request
        original_max = self.trainer.max_training_hours
        self.trainer.max_training_hours = duration_hours
        
        try:
            result = self.trainer.start_training_session(focus_areas)
            return result
        finally:
            # Restore original max
            self.trainer.max_training_hours = original_max
    
    def _start_training_monitor(self):
        """Start thread to monitor and schedule training"""
        def monitor_loop():
            while True:
                try:
                    # Check schedule
                    self.scheduler.check_and_start_training()
                    
                    # Check for system idle (for idle training)
                    # This would be more sophisticated in production
                    
                    time.sleep(60)  # Check every minute
                    
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.error(f"Training monitor error: {e}")
                    time.sleep(300)  # Wait 5 minutes on error
        
        thread = threading.Thread(target=monitor_loop, daemon=True, name="Training_Monitor")
        thread.start()

class TrainingReportGenerator:
    """Generate training reports"""
    
    def generate_report(self, training_history: List[TrainingSession],
                       improvement_log: ImprovementLog,
                       days: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Generate comprehensive training report"""
        
        # Filter to requested time period
        cutoff = time.time() - (days * 24 * 3600)
        recent_sessions = [s for s in training_history if s.end_time and s.end_time > cutoff]
        recent_improvements = [i for i in improvement_log.improvements 
                              if i["timestamp"] > cutoff]
        
        # Calculate metrics
        total_training_time = sum(s.end_time - s.start_time for s in recent_sessions)
        avg_session_duration = total_training_time / len(recent_sessions) if recent_sessions else 0
        
        # Group improvements by type
        improvements_by_type = defaultdict(list)
        for imp in recent_improvements:
            improvements_by_type[imp.get("type", "unknown")].append(imp)
        
        # Calculate impact scores
        impact_scores = {}
        for imp_type, imps in improvements_by_type.items():
            total_impact = sum(imp.get("impact", 0) for imp in imps if isinstance(imp.get("impact"), (int, float)))
            impact_scores[imp_type] = {
                "count": len(imps),
                "total_impact": total_impact,
                "avg_impact": total_impact / len(imps) if imps else 0
            }
        
        # Generate insights
        insights = self._generate_insights(recent_sessions, recent_improvements)
        
        report = {
            "period_days": days,
            "summary": {
                "sessions": len(recent_sessions),
                "total_training_hours": total_training_time / 3600,
                "avg_session_hours": avg_session_duration / 3600,
                "improvements": len(recent_improvements)
            },
            "performance_metrics": {
                "response_time_change": self._calculate_performance_change("response_time", recent_sessions),
                "accuracy_change": self._calculate_performance_change("accuracy", recent_sessions),
                "efficiency_change": self._calculate_performance_change("efficiency", recent_sessions)
            },
            "improvements_breakdown": dict(impact_scores),
            "insights": insights,
            "recommendations": self._generate_recommendations(recent_sessions, recent_improvements)
        }
        
        return report
    
    def _generate_insights(self, sessions: List[TrainingSession], 
                          improvements: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[str]:
        """Generate insights from training data"""
        insights = []
        
        if not sessions:
            return ["No training sessions in this period"]
        
        # Find most productive training times
        session_times = [(s.start_time % 86400) / 3600 for s in sessions]  # Hour of day
        if session_times:
            avg_hour = sum(session_times) / len(session_times)
            insights.append(f"Most training occurs around {int(avg_hour):02d}:00")
        
        # Identify most improved areas
        improvement_areas = defaultdict(int)
        for imp in improvements:
            area = imp.get("impact", "general")
            if isinstance(area, str):
                improvement_areas[area] += imp.get("impact_value", 1)
        
        if improvement_areas:
            best_area = max(improvement_areas.items(), key=lambda x: x[1])
            insights.append(f"Most improved area: {best_area[0]} ({best_area[1]:.1f}% improvement)")
        
        # Learning rate insight
        if len(sessions) > 3:
            early_sessions = sessions[:3]
            late_sessions = sessions[-3:]
            
            early_improvements = sum(len(s.improvements) for s in early_sessions)
            late_improvements = sum(len(s.improvements) for s in late_sessions)
            
            if early_improvements > 0:
                improvement_rate = late_improvements / early_improvements
                insights.append(f"Learning rate: {improvement_rate:.2f}x improvement over period")
        
        return insights

# ===== INTEGRATION WITH EXISTING HELENA =====

def integrate_training_system(helena_kernel, helena_runtime, helena_memory):
    """Integrate training system with existing HELENA"""
    
    # Create training interface
    training_interface = HELENATrainingInterface(
        helena_kernel,
        helena_runtime,
        helena_memory
    )
    
    # Add training commands to kernel
    helena_kernel.training_system = training_interface
    
    # Add training status to dashboard
    def get_training_dashboard():
        status = training_interface.get_training_status()
        report = training_interface.get_improvement_report(7)
        
        return {
            "training_status": status,
            "weekly_report": report
        }
    
    # Monkey-patch to add training capabilities
    # In production, would use proper dependency injection
    
    return training_interface

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Example of setting up HELENA with autonomous training
    
    # 1. Initialize HELENA components (from existing system)
    kernel = HELENAKernel("primary_operator")
    runtime = HELENARuntime()
    memory = HELENAMemory()
    
    # 2. Integrate training system
    training = integrate_training_system(kernel, runtime, memory)
    
    # 3. Setup autonomous training with operator preferences
    operator_token = "secure_operator_token_123"
    preferences = {
        "daily": {
            "time": "03:00",  # 3 AM daily
            "duration": "1.5h",
            "enabled": True
        },
        "focus_areas": ["code_quality", "response_time", "memory_efficiency"],
        "security_level": "high"
    }
    
    result = training.setup_autonomous_training(operator_token, preferences)
    print("Training setup result:", json.dumps(result, indent=2))
    
    # 4. Check training status periodically
    time.sleep(60)
    status = training.get_training_status()
    print("Training status:", json.dumps(status, indent=2))
    
    # 5. Manual training request example
    manual_result = training.manual_training_request(
        focus_areas=["security_auditing", "feedback_loop_detection"],
        duration_hours=0.5
    )
    print("Manual training started:", manual_result)
KEY FEATURES OF THIS SELF-TRAINING SYSTEM
1. Autonomous Learning Cycles:
Scheduled Training: Daily/Weekly automatic sessions

Idle-Time Training: Uses system idle time opportunistically

Manual Override: Operator can trigger training anytime

2. Security-First Training:
Pre-Training Audits: All training data validated before use

Improvement Validation: Each improvement security-checked

Rollback Capability: Automatic restoration if issues detected

Parameter Constraints: Limits on how much HELENA can change itself

3. Feedback Loop Recognition:
Loop Detection: Identifies positive/negative feedback loops

Pattern Analysis: Recognizes recurring decision patterns

Self-Correction: Automatically breaks harmful loops

Amplification: Strengthens beneficial loops

4. Software Engineering Self-Improvement:
Code Pattern Learning: Learns from successful code generations

Error Analysis: Studies failures to prevent recurrence

Style Adaptation: Adapts to operator coding preferences

Optimization Discovery: Identifies and implements optimizations

5. Continuous Improvement Metrics:
Performance Tracking: Monitors response times, accuracy, efficiency

Improvement Logging: Records all changes with impact assessment

Learning Rate Analysis: Measures how quickly HELENA improves

Regression Detection: Alerts if changes cause performance decline

6. Operator Control & Transparency:
Explicit Enablement: Training requires operator authorization

Preference Settings: Operator defines focus areas and schedule

Comprehensive Reports: Detailed improvement reports

Manual Override: Operator can pause/stop training anytime

Vector DB: ChromaDB (embedded, lightweight)

Graph DB: NetworkX + custom persistence

Sandboxing: multiprocessing + resource limits + seccomp (Linux)

CPU: x86_64, ARM64 (Apple Silicon/Raspberry Pi)

RAM: 12GB minimum, 32GB recommended

Storage: 20GB minimum, SSD strongly recommended

ML Model Strategy:
Primary: Mistral 7B Instruct (4-bit quantized) - 4.5GB

Embeddings: all-MiniLM-L6-v2 (80MB)

Code Generation: StarCoder 3B (2GB) or CodeLlama 7B

Fallback: DistilBERT for low-memory systems

CORE ARCHITECTURE DECISIONS
1. KERNEL DESIGN
Multi-threaded event loop with priority queues

Four operational modes with distinct processing pipelines

Permission matrix tied to operational mode

Validation chains for all outputs (3-pass minimum)

Personality injection at response formatting layer

Learning hooks after every successful execution

2. MEMORY SYSTEM
Three-tier storage:

Working memory (LRU cache, 1,000 items)
Short-term memory (vector store, 100,000 items)
Long-term memory (compressed, encrypted archives)
Dual indexing: Vector + Graph

Contextual retrieval with temporal weighting

Automatic memory grooming (pruning, deduplication, compression)

3. RUNTIME CONTROL
Hardware abstraction layer with plugin architecture

Dynamic resource allocation based on:

System load detection

Thermal conditions

Operator preferences

Task priority

Gaming mode:

Automatic detection (GPU load + foreground process)

Graceful degradation of non-critical services

Manual override available

4. SECURITY ARCHITECTURE
Defense in depth:

Process isolation (sandboxes)
Memory encryption (AES-256-GCM)
System call filtering (seccomp/bpf)
Network egress control
Kill switch:

Hardware token requirement (optional)

7-stage shutdown (DoD standard wiping)

Recovery lockdown (72-hour cooldown)

5. MODULE SYSTEM
Hot-loadable with dependency resolution

Three isolation levels:

Full sandbox (untrusted)
Limited sandbox (certified)
Trusted execution (built-in)
Resource quotas enforced by cgroups/Job Objects

Digital signatures for all third-party modules

python
# helena_core/utils/config_manager.py
"""
Centralized configuration management with encryption and validation
"""
import os
import yaml
import json
import hashlib
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, Union
from dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict
from enum import Enum
import logging

from cryptography.fernet import Fernet
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.pbkdf2 import PBKDF2HMAC
import base64

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class ConfigSection(Enum):
    """Configuration sections"""
    SYSTEM = "system"
    PERFORMANCE = "performance"
    MEMORY = "memory"
    SECURITY = "security"
    NETWORK = "network"
    PERSONALITY = "personality"
    TRAINING = "training"
    MODULES = "modules"

@dataclass
class SystemConfig:
    """System-level configuration"""
    name: str = "HELENA"
    version: str = "1.0.0"
    operator_id: str = "primary_operator"
    log_level: str = "INFO"
    data_directory: str = "./helena_data"
    temp_directory: str = "./helena_temp"
    max_log_size_mb: int = 100
    log_retention_days: int = 30
    
@dataclass
class PerformanceConfig:
    """Performance configuration"""
    default_profile: str = "normal"
    auto_throttle: bool = True
    gaming_mode_auto: bool = True
    cpu_idle_threshold: float = 30.0  # Percent
    thermal_threshold: float = 85.0   # Celsius
    response_time_target_ms: int = 1000
    
    # Resource limits
    cpu_limit_normal: float = 50.0    # Percent
    cpu_limit_background: float = 25.0
    cpu_limit_turbo: float = 80.0
    
    ram_limit_normal_mb: int = 4096
    ram_limit_background_mb: int = 2048
    ram_limit_turbo_mb: int = 8192
    
@dataclass  
class MemoryConfig:
    """Memory system configuration"""
    vector_dimension: int = 768
    max_working_memories: int = 1000
    max_short_term_memories: int = 100000
    cache_size: int = 1000
    embedding_model: str = "all-MiniLM-L6-v2"
    similarity_threshold: float = 0.7
    auto_cleanup_interval_hours: int = 24
    
@dataclass
class SecurityConfig:
    """Security configuration"""
    encryption_enabled: bool = True
    encryption_algorithm: str = "AES-256-GCM"
    require_validation: bool = True
    max_unauthorized_attempts: int = 5
    sandbox_enabled: bool = True
    network_require_approval: bool = True
    kill_switch_hardware_token: Optional[str] = None
    
@dataclass
class PersonalityConfig:
    """Personality configuration"""
    verbosity: float = 0.4            # 0-1 scale
    technical_depth: float = 0.8
    humor_threshold: float = 0.7
    creativity_level: float = 0.6
    formality_level: float = 0.8
    response_style: str = "concise_technical"
    
@dataclass
class TrainingConfig:
    """Training system configuration"""
    enabled: bool = False
    max_training_hours: float = 2.0
    scheduled_time: str = "02:00"     # 2 AM
    focus_areas: list = field(default_factory=lambda: ["code_quality", "efficiency"])
    max_parameter_change: float = 0.1  # 10%
    require_operator_approval: bool = True
    
@dataclass
class ModuleConfig:
    """Module system configuration"""
    sandbox_default: bool = True
    max_cpu_percent: float = 25.0
    max_memory_mb: int = 512
    network_access_default: bool = False
    filesystem_access_default: str = "sandbox_only"
    require_digital_signature: bool = True
    
@dataclass
class HelenaConfig:
    """Complete HELENA configuration"""
    system: SystemConfig = field(default_factory=SystemConfig)
    performance: PerformanceConfig = field(default_factory=PerformanceConfig)
    memory: MemoryConfig = field(default_factory=MemoryConfig)
    security: SecurityConfig = field(default_factory=SecurityConfig)
    personality: PersonalityConfig = field(default_factory=PersonalityConfig)
    training: TrainingConfig = field(default_factory=TrainingConfig)
    modules: ModuleConfig = field(default_factory=ModuleConfig)
    
    # Runtime state (not saved)
    _encryption_key: Optional[bytes] = None
    _config_hash: Optional[str] = None
    _loaded_path: Optional[Path] = None

class ConfigManager:
    """Manages HELENA configuration with encryption and validation"""
    
    def __init__(self, config_path: Optional[Path] = None):
        self.config_path = config_path or Path.home() / ".helena" / "config"
        self.config_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        
        self.config = HelenaConfig()
        self.fernet = None
        
        # Default hardware profiles path
        self.hardware_profiles_path = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "config" / "hardware_profiles.yaml"
        self.security_policies_path = Path(__file__).parent.parent / "config" / "security_policies.yaml"
        
    def initialize(self, operator_id: str, encryption_key: Optional[bytes] = None) -> bool:
        """
        Initialize configuration system
        Returns: True if successful
        """
        try:
            # Set operator ID
            self.config.system.operator_id = operator_id
            
            # Generate or set encryption key
            if encryption_key:
                self.config._encryption_key = encryption_key
            elif self.config.security.encryption_enabled:
                self.config._encryption_key = self._generate_encryption_key(operator_id)
            
            # Initialize encryption
            if self.config._encryption_key:
                self.fernet = Fernet(self._derive_fernet_key(self.config._encryption_key))
            
            # Load or create config
            if self.config_path.exists():
                loaded = self.load()
                if not loaded:
                    logger.warning("Failed to load config, creating default")
                    return self._create_default_config()
                return True
            else:
                return self._create_default_config()
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to initialize config: {e}")
            return False
    
    def _create_default_config(self) -> bool:
        """Create default configuration file"""
        try:
            # Detect hardware and apply profile
            hardware_profile = self._detect_hardware_profile()
            self._apply_hardware_profile(hardware_profile)
            
            # Save config
            return self.save()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to create default config: {e}")
            return False
    
    def _detect_hardware_profile(self) -> str:
        """Detect hardware and return appropriate profile name"""
        try:
            import psutil
            cpu_cores = psutil.cpu_count(logical=False)
            total_ram = psutil.virtual_memory().total / (1024**3)  # GB
            
            # Simple profile detection
            if total_ram < 8:
                return "minimal"
            elif total_ram < 16:
                return "standard"
            elif total_ram < 32:
                return "performance"
            else:
                return "workstation"
                
        except Exception:
            return "standard"
    
    def _apply_hardware_profile(self, profile_name: str):
        """Apply hardware-specific configuration"""
        try:
            if self.hardware_profiles_path.exists():
                with open(self.hardware_profiles_path, 'r') as f:
                    profiles = yaml.safe_load(f)
                
                profile = profiles.get(profile_name, {})
                
                # Apply profile settings
                if "performance" in profile:
                    perf = profile["performance"]
                    self.config.performance.cpu_limit_normal = perf.get("cpu_limit_normal", 50.0)
                    self.config.performance.ram_limit_normal_mb = perf.get("ram_limit_normal_mb", 4096)
                
                if "memory" in profile:
                    mem = profile["memory"]
                    self.config.memory.max_working_memories = mem.get("max_working_memories", 1000)
                    self.config.memory.max_short_term_memories = mem.get("max_short_term_memories", 100000)
                    
                logger.info(f"Applied hardware profile: {profile_name}")
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Failed to apply hardware profile: {e}")
    
    def load(self) -> bool:
        """Load configuration from encrypted file"""
        try:
            if not self.config_path.exists():
                return False
            
            with open(self.config_path, 'rb') as f:
                encrypted_data = f.read()
            
            # Decrypt if encryption enabled
            if self.config.security.encryption_enabled and self.fernet:
                try:
                    decrypted_data = self.fernet.decrypt(encrypted_data)
                    config_dict = yaml.safe_load(decrypted_data.decode('utf-8'))
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.error(f"Failed to decrypt config: {e}")
                    return False
            else:
                config_dict = yaml.safe_load(encrypted_data.decode('utf-8'))
            
            # Update config object
            self._update_from_dict(config_dict)
            
            # Store hash for change detection
            self.config._config_hash = self._calculate_config_hash()
            self.config._loaded_path = self.config_path
            
            logger.info("Configuration loaded successfully")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to load config: {e}")
            return False
    
    def save(self) -> bool:
        """Save configuration to encrypted file"""
        try:
            # Convert config to dict
            config_dict = self._to_dict()
            
            # Serialize to YAML
            yaml_data = yaml.dump(config_dict, default_flow_style=False)
            
            # Encrypt if enabled
            if self.config.security.encryption_enabled and self.fernet:
                encrypted_data = self.fernet.encrypt(yaml_data.encode('utf-8'))
            else:
                encrypted_data = yaml_data.encode('utf-8')
            
            # Create backup if file exists
            if self.config_path.exists():
                backup_path = self.config_path.with_suffix('.bak')
                import shutil
                shutil.copy2(self.config_path, backup_path)
            
            # Write to file
            with open(self.config_path, 'wb') as f:
                f.write(encrypted_data)
            
            # Update hash
            self.config._config_hash = self._calculate_config_hash()
            
            logger.info("Configuration saved successfully")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to save config: {e}")
            return False
    
    def get_section(self, section: ConfigSection) -> Any:
        """Get configuration section"""
        section_map = {
            ConfigSection.SYSTEM: self.config.system,
            ConfigSection.PERFORMANCE: self.config.performance,
            ConfigSection.MEMORY: self.config.memory,
            ConfigSection.SECURITY: self.config.security,
            ConfigSection.PERSONALITY: self.config.personality,
            ConfigSection.TRAINING: self.config.training,
            ConfigSection.MODULES: self.config.modules,
        }
        return section_map.get(section)
    
    def update_section(self, section: ConfigSection, updates: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """Update configuration section"""
        try:
            section_obj = self.get_section(section)
            if not section_obj:
                return False
            
            # Update fields
            for key, value in updates.items():
                if hasattr(section_obj, key):
                    setattr(section_obj, key, value)
            
            # Save changes
            return self.save()
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to update config section: {e}")
            return False
    
    def validate(self) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
        """Validate configuration, return errors by section"""
        errors = {}
        
        # System validation
        system_errors = []
        if not self.config.system.operator_id or len(self.config.system.operator_id) < 3:
            system_errors.append("Operator ID must be at least 3 characters")
        if self.config.system.max_log_size_mb < 10:
            system_errors.append("Max log size must be at least 10MB")
        if system_errors:
            errors["system"] = system_errors
        
        # Performance validation
        perf_errors = []
        if not 0 <= self.config.performance.cpu_limit_normal <= 100:
            perf_errors.append("CPU limit must be between 0 and 100")
        if self.config.performance.ram_limit_normal_mb < 512:
            perf_errors.append("RAM limit must be at least 512MB")
        if perf_errors:
            errors["performance"] = perf_errors
        
        # Security validation
        sec_errors = []
        if self.config.security.encryption_enabled and not self.config._encryption_key:
            sec_errors.append("Encryption enabled but no key set")
        if sec_errors:
            errors["security"] = sec_errors
        
        return errors
    
    def get_encryption_key(self) -> Optional[bytes]:
        """Get encryption key (handle with care)"""
        return self.config._encryption_key
    
    def reset_to_defaults(self, keep_operator_id: bool = True) -> bool:
        """Reset configuration to defaults"""
        try:
            operator_id = self.config.system.operator_id if keep_operator_id else "primary_operator"
            
            # Create new config
            self.config = HelenaConfig()
            self.config.system.operator_id = operator_id
            
            # Re-initialize
            return self.initialize(operator_id, self.config._encryption_key)
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to reset config: {e}")
            return False
    
    def export_config(self, export_path: Path, include_secrets: bool = False) -> bool:
        """Export configuration to file"""
        try:
            config_dict = self._to_dict()
            
            # Remove sensitive data if requested
            if not include_secrets:
                if "_encryption_key" in config_dict:
                    del config_dict["_encryption_key"]
                if "security" in config_dict:
                    if "kill_switch_hardware_token" in config_dict["security"]:
                        del config_dict["security"]["kill_switch_hardware_token"]
            
            with open(export_path, 'w') as f:
                yaml.dump(config_dict, f, default_flow_style=False)
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to export config: {e}")
            return False
    
    def _generate_encryption_key(self, operator_id: str) -> bytes:
        """Generate encryption key from operator ID and system entropy"""
        import secrets
        
        # Use operator ID as salt
        salt = operator_id.encode('utf-8')
        
        # Generate random component
        random_component = secrets.token_bytes(32)
        
        # Combine with deterministic component from operator ID
        kdf = PBKDF2HMAC(
            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
            length=32,
            salt=salt,
            iterations=100000,
        )
        
        deterministic_component = kdf.derive(operator_id.encode('utf-8'))
        
        # XOR combine for final key
        key = bytes(a ^ b for a, b in zip(random_component, deterministic_component))
        
        return key
    
    def _derive_fernet_key(self, encryption_key: bytes) -> bytes:
        """Derive Fernet key from encryption key"""
        kdf = PBKDF2HMAC(
            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
            length=32,
            salt=b'helena_fernet_salt',
            iterations=100000,
        )
        return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(kdf.derive(encryption_key))
    
    def _to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Convert config to dictionary, excluding runtime attributes"""
        config_dict = {}
        
        # Convert each dataclass section
        for field_name in self.config.__dataclass_fields__:
            if field_name.startswith('_'):
                continue  # Skip private fields
            
            field_value = getattr(self.config, field_name)
            if hasattr(field_value, '__dataclass_fields__'):
                # It's a dataclass
                config_dict[field_name] = asdict(field_value)
            else:
                config_dict[field_name] = field_value
        
        return config_dict
    
    def _update_from_dict(self, config_dict: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Update config from dictionary"""
        for section_name, section_data in config_dict.items():
            if hasattr(self.config, section_name):
                section_obj = getattr(self.config, section_name)
                
                if hasattr(section_obj, '__dataclass_fields__'):
                    # Update dataclass fields
                    for field_name, field_value in section_data.items():
                        if hasattr(section_obj, field_name):
                            setattr(section_obj, field_name, field_value)
                else:
                    # Direct attribute
                    setattr(self.config, section_name, section_data)
    
    def _calculate_config_hash(self) -> str:
        """Calculate hash of current configuration"""
        config_dict = self._to_dict()
        config_str = json.dumps(config_dict, sort_keys=True)
        return hashlib.sha256(config_str.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    def has_changed(self) -> bool:
        """Check if config has changed since load"""
        if not self.config._config_hash:
            return True
        
        current_hash = self._calculate_config_hash()
        return current_hash != self.config._config_hash

# Singleton instance
_config_manager: Optional[ConfigManager] = None

def get_config_manager(config_path: Optional[Path] = None) -> ConfigManager:
    """Get or create configuration manager singleton"""
    global _config_manager
    if _config_manager is None:
        _config_manager = ConfigManager(config_path)
    return _config_manager
